## Purpose

This file is the authoritative final-draft version of `f081r`.

`f81r` is a Book III bath page. GRADED ENTRY — gentle carrier establishment followed by stronger processing. Simpler bath system with two distinct processing phases. First phase establishes a calm carrier fluid. Second phase re-enters with stronger circulation loop plus a single correction pulse. Fewer nymph figures than other... Two-stage routing: establish a calm carrier first, then re-enter with a stronger circulation loop and a single correction pulse to lock the state.

### Liminal

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[\bigl(p_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+, \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+, f_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+\bigr) = L_{\mathrm{P_1}}\bigl(p_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, f_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-\bigr), \qquad f_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \mathrm{Tr}(\Pi_{\mathrm{fail}}\rho_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+)\]

## Direct Operational Meaning

Two-stage routing: establish a calm carrier first, then re-enter with a stronger circulation loop and a single correction pulse to lock the state. Process statistics: 38 circulation commands (qo-); 3 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 10 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

Across the formal lenses, `f81r` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=38, N_valve=3, and N_seal=0. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).
